               <p>一位渔夫和一位<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家在一条河上相遇了。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家问:“你会外语吗？”渔夫回答:“不会。”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家又问:“你懂得历史吗？”渔夫还是回答:“不懂。”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家对渔夫说:“那你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1654">等于</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2361">失去</span>了半条生命。”突然，一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2768">阵</span>狂风<span class="label-words" data-wid="1592">吹</span>翻了小船，渔夫和<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家都掉进了河里。渔夫问<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家:“你会游泳吗？”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2760">哲学</span>家说:“不会。”渔夫说:“那你将<span class="label-words" data-wid="2361">失去</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2775">整个</span>生命。”</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>我刚开始学滑雪的时候，最大的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2461">体会</span>就是停不下来。我那时没有请<span class="label-words" data-wid="1983">教练</span>，看着别人滑雪，觉得很容易，不就是从山顶滑到山下吗？于是我穿上滑雪板，哧溜一下就滑下去了，结果我实际上是从山顶<span class="label-words" data-wid="1852">滚</span>到了山下，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2408">摔</span>了很多个跟头。我发现自己<span class="label-words" data-wid="1795">根本</span>就不知道怎么停止、怎么<span class="label-words" data-wid="1445">保持</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2230">平衡</span>。最后我<span class="label-words" data-wid="1720">反复</span>练习怎么在雪地上、<span class="label-words" data-wid="2607">斜</span>坡上停下来。练了一个星期，我终于学会了在任何坡上停止、滑行、再停止。这个时候我就发现自己会滑雪了，敢从山顶高速地往山坡下<span class="label-words" data-wid="1567">冲</span>。因为我知道只要我想停，一转身就能停下来。只要你能停下来，你就不会撞上树、撞上<span class="label-words" data-wid="2364">石头</span>、撞上人。因此，只有知道<span class="label-words" data-wid="2316">如何</span>停止的人，才知道<span class="label-words" data-wid="2316">如何</span>高速前进。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>常常有人跟我说，很想<span class="label-words" data-wid="2483">投资</span>，就是没钱。他们的误区在于，总认为<span class="label-words" data-wid="2483">投资</span>得有一大笔钱才能开始，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2483">投资</span>一次性至少也得是十万八万的，否则就没什么<span class="label-words" data-wid="2686">意义</span>。但是富人的钱也是从一块钱攒起来的，财务<span class="label-words" data-wid="2857">自由</span>不是一天就可以<span class="label-words" data-wid="2374">实现</span>的。我家的一个邻居王<span class="label-words" data-wid="2439">太太</span>，刚搬来时就在<span class="label-words" data-wid="1512">餐厅</span>里刷盘子，她把遗弃的各种废旧瓶子都积攒起来卖钱，看上去值不了几个钱的东西她也从来不放过。现在她的资产已经超过千万了，所有的积蓄都是她从不起眼的小钱<span class="label-words" data-wid="2483">投资</span>开始的。我这里并不是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1963">建议</span>大家要如此的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2239">朴素</span>，但这个经验是很有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>的，别<span class="label-words" data-wid="2049">看不起</span>它，要从小钱开始。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

                   <div id="w38-container" class="cp-container">

                     <div class="cp-buffer-1"></div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>有一个人做了一个梦，梦中，他来到一个地方。走进第一层时，他发现有一张长长的大桌子，上面<span class="label-words" data-wid="1435">摆</span>满了丰盛的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2379">食物</span>，桌子旁边都坐着人，可是没有一个人能吃得到，因为大家的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1783">胳膊</span>受到魔法师<span class="label-words" data-wid="2066">控制</span>，全都变成了直的，不能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2502">弯</span>曲，桌上的美食，也就无法吃到，所以个个愁苦满面。但是他听到楼上却<span class="label-words" data-wid="1565">充满</span>了笑声，他<span class="label-words" data-wid="1867">好奇</span>地上楼一看，同样的也有一群人，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1783">胳膊</span>也都不能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2502">弯</span>曲，但是大家却吃得兴高采烈。原来虽然他们的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1783">胳膊</span>不能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2502">弯</span>曲，但大家互相帮助夹菜喂食，结果都吃得很尽兴。在生命的道路上，没有一个人可以完全不依靠别人而<span class="label-words" data-wid="1683">独立</span>生活，先主动<span class="label-words" data-wid="2346">伸</span>出友谊的手，你会发现原来四周有这么多的朋友。</p>
              </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2839">追求</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2504">完美</span>，严格要求自己，这是一种难能可贵的品质。但是，在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2573">现实</span>生活中，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2839">追求</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2504">完美</span>是不实际的，因为世界上<span class="label-words" data-wid="1795">根本</span>没有<span class="label-words" data-wid="2504">完美</span>的人和事。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>学家指出，过度<span class="label-words" data-wid="2839">追求</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2504">完美</span>是一种不健康的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>，这样的人往往会以自我为<span class="label-words" data-wid="2806">中心</span>，从自己的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1979">角度</span>去要求和判断别人。长期下去，不仅让周围的人<span class="label-words" data-wid="1553">承受</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2027">巨大</span>压力，影响人际交往，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2474">同时</span>也不利于自己的身心健康。所以，学会<span class="label-words" data-wid="1673">调整</span>自己的心态很重要。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

                 <div class="field-question ans-hide">

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>以前，人们跳槽的一个重要标准就是收入要有增长；而<span class="label-words" data-wid="2317">如今</span>，许多人换新的工作时，把工资的增长看得越来越<span class="label-words" data-wid="1635">淡</span>了，如果新工作有发展<span class="label-words" data-wid="2063">空间</span>、压力小、能<span class="label-words" data-wid="1707">发挥</span>自己的特长，即使收入和以前持<span class="label-words" data-wid="2225">平</span>，甚至低一点儿也无所谓。当有了一定的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2553">物质</span>基础之后，工作就有了新的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2686">意义</span>，或者是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2374">实现</span>自我<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>，或者是能给自己带来快乐。</p>

             <div class="field-heading">

              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　有一天，老虎抓住一只狐狸，心想，今天可以美美地<span class="child-number">46</span>一顿午餐了。狐狸很<span class="label-words" data-wid="1981">狡猾</span>，骗老虎说:“我是天帝<span class="label-words" data-wid="2204">派</span>到山林中来做百兽之王的，你<span class="label-words" data-wid="2658">要是</span>吃了我，天帝是不会原谅你的。”老虎问:“你是百兽之王，有什么<span class="child-number">47</span>？”狐狸<span class="label-words" data-wid="2103">连忙</span>说:“你如果不相信我的话，可以随我到山林中去走一走，我让你亲眼看看百兽害怕我的样子。”</p> 
               <p>老虎想这倒也是个办法，<span class="child-number">48</span>，自己尾随其后，一起向山林深处走去。森林中的动物们远远地看见老虎来了，都<span class="child-number">49</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2444">逃</span>命。老虎不知道动物们是害怕自己而<span class="label-words" data-wid="2444">逃</span>跑的，还以为它们是害怕狐狸才<span class="label-words" data-wid="2444">逃</span>走的。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

               <p>　　“欲速则不达”，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2303">人生</span>不能一味<span class="label-words" data-wid="2839">追求</span>速度，其实“慢”也是一种生活的艺术。“慢工出细活”，这里的“慢”并不意味着低<span class="child-number">57</span>，而是指按计划逐步进行工作，才能<span class="label-words" data-wid="1612">达到</span>好的效果。说话也要学会“慢”。有的人好发<span class="label-words" data-wid="2683">议论</span>，不<span class="label-words" data-wid="2332">善于</span>克制自己，很多话不经<span class="child-number">58</span>脱口而出，带来不<span class="label-words" data-wid="1465">必要</span>的麻烦。现代人工作忙碌，生活节奏快，<span class="child-number">59</span>。应该试着让生活节奏放慢些，吃饭要慢慢吃，开车不要超速，不要每件事都跟别人竞争，也<span class="label-words" data-wid="1489">不必</span>每日加班……现代人要想<span class="child-number">60</span>身心健康，要学会“慢”这个养生之道。</p>

              <div class="field-subject text-indent">
               <p>火箭飞向月球需要一定的速度和质量，而火箭如此庞大，是无论<span class="label-words" data-wid="2316">如何</span>也无法飞上天的。因此，很长一段时间，科学界<span class="label-words" data-wid="2669">一致</span>认定:火箭<span class="label-words" data-wid="1795">根本</span>不可能被送上月球。直到有人提出“分级火箭”的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2418">思想</span>，这一问题才得到解决。将火箭分成若干级，第一级将其他级送出大气层时<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>自行脱落以减轻质量，这样火箭的其他部分就能轻松地飞向月球了。</p>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　一只新组装好的小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>被放到了两只旧<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>跟前。两只旧<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>“滴答滴答”一分一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2160">秒</span>地走着。一只旧<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>对小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>说:“来吧，你也该工作了。可是我有点儿担心，你走完3100多万次以后，恐怕<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>吃不消了。”“天哪！ 3100多万次？ ”小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>吃惊不已，“要我做这么大的事？办不到，办不到。”但另一只旧<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>却说:“别听他<span class="label-words" data-wid="2563">瞎</span>说。不用害怕，其实你只要每<span class="label-words" data-wid="2160">秒</span>钟‘滴答’，一下就行了。”“天下哪有这样简单的事情。”小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>将信将疑。那只旧<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>说:“那你何不试试呢？”“好吧。”小<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>很轻松地开始“滴答”起来。它每<span class="label-words" data-wid="2160">秒</span>钟“滴答”一下，不知不觉中，一年过去了，它<span class="label-words" data-wid="1435">摆</span>了3100多万次。</p> 
               <p>　　每个人都希望梦想成真，成功却<span class="label-words" data-wid="2422">似乎</span>远在天边，遥不可及。倦怠和不<span class="label-words" data-wid="2856">自信</span>让我们怀疑自己的能力，最终放弃努力。其实，我们<span class="label-words" data-wid="1489">不必</span>想一年甚至一个月之后的事，只要想着今天我要做些什么，明天我该做些什么，然后努力去完成它，就像那只<span class="label-words" data-wid="2808">钟</span>一样，每<span class="label-words" data-wid="2160">秒</span>“滴答”一下，成功的喜悦就会慢慢渗入我们的生命。</p>
              </div>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　新<span class="label-words" data-wid="2641">学期</span>开始时，校长把三位老师叫进办公室，对他们说:“根据你们过去的教学<span class="label-words" data-wid="1479">表现</span>，你们是本校最优秀的教师。因此，我们<span class="label-words" data-wid="2451">特意</span>挑选了全校最聪明的100名学生组成三个班让你们教。这些学生比别的孩子都要聪明，希望你们能让他们取得更好的成绩。”三位老师都高兴地表示一定<span class="label-words" data-wid="2010">尽力</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　校长又叮嘱他们，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1692">对待</span>这些孩子，要像<span class="label-words" data-wid="2226">平常</span>一样，不要让孩子或家长知道他们是被<span class="label-words" data-wid="2451">特意</span>挑选出来的。老师们都<span class="label-words" data-wid="1613">答应</span>了。一年之后，这三个班的学生成绩果然排在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2775">整个</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>的前列。这时，校长告诉了老师真相:这些学生并不是刻意选出来的最优秀的学生，只不过是随机抽调的普通学生。老师们没想到会是这样，经过<span class="label-words" data-wid="1742">分析</span>，他们都认为自己的教学水平高才是真正的原因。这时校长又告诉他们另一个真相，那就是，他们也不是被专门挑选出来的全校最优秀的教师，也只是随机抽调的普通老师。</p>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　一位科学家跟一位<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人搭<span class="label-words" data-wid="1555">乘</span>同一列火车，两人互不相识。因为很无聊，科学家对<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人说:“你要不要跟我玩儿个游戏？”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人看了看科学家，没有搭腔。科学家继续说:“我是科学家，我们互相问<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>问题，答不出来的要给5块钱，怎么样？”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人想自己不太容易赢科学家，于是委婉地拒绝了。科学家仍不死心:“这样好了，你答不出来只要给我5块钱，如果我答不出来，就给你50块，这样可以了吧？”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人于是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1613">答应</span>了他。科学家问:“地球到月亮之间有多少公里？”<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人答不出来，直接拿了5块给科学家。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1991">接着</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人问:“什么东西上山时是四条腿，下山时是五条腿？”科学家迷惑地看着<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人，拿出了几张纸，开始在上面<span class="label-words" data-wid="1929">计算</span>着，一直到火车到站的时候，他也没算出答案是什么，只好拿了50块给<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人。科学家最后<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>问:“那答案是什么？告诉我吧。” 只见<span class="label-words" data-wid="2363">诗</span>人耸耸肩，拿了5块钱给他，然后得意地走了。</p>

             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ2 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">83-86</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               83-86
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　有一位青年去求职，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2691">应聘</span>几家<span class="label-words" data-wid="1630">单位</span>都被拒之门外，感到十分沮丧。最后，他抱着一线希望又去一家公司<span class="label-words" data-wid="2691">应聘</span>。在此之前，他先去<span class="label-words" data-wid="1617">打听</span>了该公司老总的历史。通过了解，发现这个公司老总以前也有与自己相似的经历。他如获珍宝，在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2691">应聘</span>时，他就与老总畅谈自己的求职经历，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2679">以及</span>自己怀才不遇的愤慨。果然，这一席话博得了老总的赏识和同情，最终他被录用为<span class="label-words" data-wid="2659">业务</span>经理。</p> 
               <p>　　这就是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2433">所谓</span>的“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>效应”，即两个人在交往时，如果首先<span class="label-words" data-wid="1477">表明</span>自己与<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>的态度和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>观相同，就会使<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>感到你与他有很多的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2581">相似</span>性，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1599">从而</span>很快地<span class="label-words" data-wid="2429">缩小</span>与你的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span>距离，更愿意同你<span class="label-words" data-wid="1989">接近</span>，结成<span class="label-words" data-wid="2108">良好</span>的人际关系。在这里，有意识、有目的地向<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1477">表明</span>态度和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1831">观点</span>，就如同<span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>一样，可以把自己介绍给<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>。</p> 
               <p>　　恰当地使用“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>”，可以尽快促成人际关系的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1961">建立</span>。但要使“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>”起到应有的作用，首先，要<span class="label-words" data-wid="2332">善于</span>捕捉<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2614">信息</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1433">把握</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2764">真实</span>的态度，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2644">寻找</span>其积极的、你可以接受的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1831">观点</span>，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2801">制作</span>一张有效的“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>”；其次，<span class="label-words" data-wid="2644">寻找</span>时机，恰到好处地向<span class="label-words" data-wid="1693">对方</span>出示你的“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>”。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2754">掌握</span>“<span class="label-words" data-wid="2609">心理</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2163">名片</span>”的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2692">应用</span>艺术，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1696">对于</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1582">处理</span>好人际关系具有很大的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2378">实用</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">
              <div class="field-children">

                 <div class="field-number">
                  84

           <div class="item">
            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="9345" data-lid="93" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="24">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ2 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">87-90</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               87-90
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>　　一家大公司的一位高级负责人因为工作失误，给公司<span class="label-words" data-wid="2741">造成</span>了1000万元的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2426">损失</span>，这件事对他打击非常大。</p> 
               <p>　　几天后，这位负责人接到了董事长接见的通知。在办公室里，他被告知调任同等重要的一个新职务。这一结果大大出乎他的意料，他十分惊讶地问道:“董事长，我犯了如此重大的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>，您为何不把我开除或降职？”</p> 
               <p>　　“如果那样<span class="label-words" data-wid="1582">处理</span>的话，岂不是在你身上白花了1000万元的‘学费’？”董事长回答说。</p> 
               <p>　　谈话还不到10分钟，却给了这位高级负责人极大的鼓励和<span class="label-words" data-wid="2349">深刻</span>的教育。他在以后的工作中，以惊人的毅力和<span class="label-words" data-wid="2804">智慧</span>为公司的发展立下了汗马功劳。</p> 
               <p>　　在这个世界上，还没有不犯<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>的人，谁都希望自己犯了<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>之后能得到别人的原谅。原谅别人就是信任别人，把他能够做的事交给他继续做下去。不信任的原谅，其实还算不上真正的原谅。信任是最好的原谅。</p> 
               <p>　　“只有一个方法，可以使过去的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>成为有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>和<span class="label-words" data-wid="1962">建设</span>性的经历，那就是冷静地<span class="label-words" data-wid="1742">分析</span>我们过去的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>。因<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>而获益，然后忘记<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>。”董事长说，“我们允许下属出错，如果哪个人在犯过几次<span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>之后变得‘茁壮’了，在公司<span class="label-words" data-wid="2050">看来</span>是很有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>的。”</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">

        var paperDate = new Date(), stopOffsetDate, timeLeft = 7200, timeTotal = 7200;
        paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + 7200);
        $('#paper-countdown').on('click', '.btn[data-op]', function () {
            var op = $(this).data('op');
            if(op === 'start' && stopOffsetDate){
                paperDate = new Date();
                paperDate.setHours(paperDate.getHours() + stopOffsetDate.hours);
                paperDate.setMinutes(paperDate.getMinutes() + stopOffsetDate.minutes);
                paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + stopOffsetDate.seconds);
                $('#paper-countdown').countdown('setFinalDate', paperDate);
            }
            $('#paper-countdown').countdown(op).find('.btn[data-op]').toggleClass('hide');
            $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('resetTime');
        }).countdown(paperDate, function (event) {
            timeLeft = event.offset.hours * 60 * 60 + event.offset.minutes * 60 + event.offset.seconds;
            $('.cd-time', this).html(event.strftime('%H:%M:%S'));
        }).on('stoped.countdown', function (event) {
            stopOffsetDate = event.offset;
        });
        $('#exercise-list').on('slid.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            var $el = $(e.relatedTarget), index = $el.index();
            $('#exr-prev').prop('disabled', $el.prev().length === 0);
            if ($el.next().length > 0) {
                $('#exr-next').removeClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').addClass('hide');
            } else {
                $('#exr-next').addClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').removeClass('hide');
            }
            if (!$el.data('autoPlayed')) {
                $el.find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
                $el.data('autoPlayed', 1);
            } else if (e.direction === 'left') {
                $el.prev().stopPlay();
            } else {
                $el.next().stopPlay();
            }
            $(this).exerciseTest('setSubmitParams', 'recent_index', index);
            activeAnswerSheetPanel(index);
        }).on('slide.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            $('.item.active .exercise-view', this).trigger('next.hsk.test');
        }).on('beforeSubmit', function (e) {
            e.submitParams.duration = timeTotal - timeLeft;
        });
        $('#exr-submit').on('click', function (e) {
            if(window.confirm('确定要提交试卷吗?')){
                $('.item.active > .exercise-view', '#exercise-list').trigger('next.hsk.test');
                $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('submit', true).done(function (data) {
                    window.location.href = '/vi/5/4/report?pid=' + data.exam_id;
                });
            }
        });
        function activeAnswerSheetPanel(index) {
            var $collapse = $('li[data-slide-to=' + index + ']', '#answer-sheets').closest('.collapse');
            if (!$collapse.hasClass('in')) {
                $collapse.prev('.panel-heading').find('[data-toggle=collapse]').trigger('click');
            }
        }
        activeAnswerSheetPanel(0);
        window.setTimeout(function () {
            $('.item.active', '#exercise-list').data('autoPlayed', 1).find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
        }, 1000);

jQuery('#emw-34fcb4d5').on('show.bs.modal', function(event){
    if(event.relatedTarget){
        var el = $(event.relatedTarget), url = el.attr('href') || el.data('url'), frm = $('iframe', this), 
        self = $(this), e = $.Event('beforeLoading.wm', {relatedTarget: el, url: url, loadingUrl : url});
        self.trigger(e);
        if(frm.data('_url') !== e.url){
            var title = el.data('title') || el.attr('title');
            title && $('.modal-title', this).html(title);
            frm.attr('src', e.loadingUrl).data('_url', e.url).parent().addClass('loading');
            self.trigger('afterLoading.wm', e.loadingUrl);
        }
    }
}).find('iframe').on('load', function() {
    $(this).height($(this.contentDocument).height()).parent().removeClass('loading');
});
